      size=3 face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.15pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly; tab-stops: 115.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">递</SPAN>延<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>益<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">3</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 10.55pt 6pt 26.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; tab-stops: 136.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>贷：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">管</SPAN>理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">费</SPAN>用<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">3</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">如果本例中甲企业选择按总额法对此类政府补助进行会计处理，则应当在确认相关管理费用的期间，借记<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>递延收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目，贷记<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>其他收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目。 
如果甲企业在取得补助资金时暂时无法确定能否满足政府补助所附条件（即在未来<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 
</SPAN>年内注册地址不得迁离本地区），则应当将收到的补助资金先计入<SPAN lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>其他应付款<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目，待客观情况 表明其能够满足政府补助所附条件后再转入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>递延收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">用于补偿企业已发生的相关成本费用或损失的，直接计入当期损益或冲减相关成本。这类</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">补助通常与企业已经发生的行为有关，是对企业已发生的成本费用或损失的补偿，或是对企业过</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">去行为的奖励。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><A 
name=_Hlk37487241><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 6</SPAN>】乙企业销售其自主开发的软件。按照国家有关规定，该企业的这种产品适用增值税 即征即退政策，按<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 16%</SPAN>的税率征收增值税后，对其增值税实际税负超过<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
3%</SPAN>的部分，实行即征即退。乙企业<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×l8 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 8 
</SPAN>月在进行纳税申报时，对归属于<SPAN lang=EN-US> 7 </SPAN>月的增值税即征即退提交退税申请，经主管 
税务机关审核后的退税额为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 </SPAN>万元。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></A></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37487241"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本例中，软件企业即征即退增值税与企业日常销售密切相关，属于与企业的日常活动相关的政府补助。乙企业<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2×18 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 8 </SPAN>月申请退税并确定了增值税退税额，账务处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 125.95pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37487241"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">其</SPAN>他<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">应</SPAN>收款<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>10<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>00<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 47.1pt; tab-stops: 136.5pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37487241"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>贷：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">其</SPAN>他<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>益<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">1</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">0</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37487241"></SPAN>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 7</SPAN>】丙企业<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 11 
</SPAN>月遭受重大自然灾害，并于<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 12 
</SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 </SPAN>日收到了政府补助资金<SPAN lang=EN-US> 200 
</SPAN>万元用于弥补其遭受自然灾害的损失。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">2×17 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 12 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 20 
</SPAN>日，丙企业实际收到补助资金并对此类补助选择按总额法进行会计处理，其账务处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 115.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">银</SPAN>行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">存</SPAN>款<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">2</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 47.1pt; tab-stops: 141.65pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>贷：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">营</SPAN>业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">外</SPAN>收入<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>200<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>00<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><A 
name=_Hlk37510837><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 
8</SPAN>】丁企业是集芳烃技术研发、生产于一体的高新技术企业。芳烃的原料是石脑油。石脑油按成品油项目在生产环节征消费税。根据国家有关规定，对使用燃料油、石脑油生产乙烯芳烃的企业购进并用于生产乙烯、芳烃类化工产品的石脑油、燃料油，按实际耗用数量退还所含消费税。假设丁企业石脑油单价为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>5333 </SPAN>元<SPAN lang=EN-US>/</SPAN>吨<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>(</SPAN>其中，消费税<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2105 </SPAN>元<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>/</SPAN>吨）。<SPAN lang=EN-US>2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>7</SPAN>月，丁企业将<SPAN lang=EN-US> 115 </SPAN>吨石脑油投入生产，石脑油转换率为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 1.15:1</SPAN>（即<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1.15 </SPAN>吨石脑油可生产<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>吨乙烯芳烃），共生产乙烯芳烃<SPAN lang=EN-US> 100 
</SPAN>吨。丁企业根据当期产量及所购原料供应商的消费税证明，向税务机关申请退还相应的消费税。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></A></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37510837"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本例中，丁企业当期应退消费税为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 
100×l.15×2105=242075(</SPAN>元）。丁企业在期末结转存货成本和主营业务成本之前，对该政府补助的账务处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 125.95pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37510837"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">其</SPAN>他<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">应</SPAN>收款<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>24<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">20</SPAN>75<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 47.1pt; tab-stops: 136.5pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37510837"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>贷：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">生</SPAN>产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">成</SPAN>本<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">2</SPAN>420<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">7</SPAN>5<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk37510837"></SPAN>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_bookmark156></A><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（三）政府补助退回的会计处理</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本准则规定，已确认的政府补助需要退回的，应当在需要退回的当期分情况按照以下规定进行会计处理：（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）初始确认时冲减相关资产账面价值的，调整资产账面价值；（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）存在相关递延</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">收益的，冲减相关递延收益账面余额，超出部分计入当期损益；（</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>3</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">）属于其他情况的，直接计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">此外，对于属于前期差错的政府补助退回，应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>28 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">会计政策、</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">会计估计变更和差错更正》作为前期差错更正进行追溯调整。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 9</SPAN>】承〖例<SPAN lang=EN-US> 4</SPAN>〗，假设<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×19 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 
</SPAN>月，因客观环境改变丁企业不再符合申请补助的条件，有关部门要求丁企业全额退回补助款。丁企业于当月退回了补助款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
210 </SPAN>万元。丁企业的账务处理如下：方法一：丁企业选择总额法对此类补助进行会计处理 
丁企业应当结转尚未分配的递延收益，并将超出部分计入当期损益。因为本例中该项补助与日常活动相关，所以这部分退回的补助冲减应退回当期的其他收益。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2×19 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 </SPAN>月丁企业退回补助款时：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.2pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 5pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN

face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>

<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 10</SPAN>】甲企业于<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 11 
</SPAN>月与某开发区政府签订合作协议，在开发区内投资设立生产基地。协议约定，开发区政府自协议签订之日起<SPAN lang=EN-US> 6 
</SPAN>个月内向甲企业提供<SPAN lang=EN-US> 300 
</SPAN>万元产业补贴资金，用于奖励该企业在开发区内投资并开展经营活动，甲企业自获得补贴起<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 
</SPAN>年内注册地址不得迁离 
本区。如果甲企业在此期限内提前迁离开发区，开发区政府允许甲企业按照实际留在本区的时间保留部分补贴，并按剩余时间追回补贴资金。甲企业于<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2×18</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1</SPAN>月<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>3</SPAN>日收到补贴资金。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">假设甲企业在实际收到补助资金时，客观情况表明甲企业在未来<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 5 </SPAN>年内迁离开发区的可能性很小，甲企业在收到补助资金时应当计入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>递延收益<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目。由于协议约定如果甲企业提前迁离开发区，开发区政府有权按扣除实际留在本区时间后的剩余时间追回部分补助，说明企业每留在 
开发区内一年，就有权取得与这一年相关的补助，与这一年补助有关的不确定性基本消除，补贴收益得以实现，所以甲企业应当将该补助在<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 
</SPAN>年内平均摊销结转计入损益。本例中，开发区政府对甲企业的补助是对该企业在开发区内投资并开展经营活动的奖励，并不指定用于补偿特定的成本费用。甲企业的账务处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">(1)2<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">×</SPAN>18<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">年<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt"> </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> </SPAN></SPAN>月<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt"> </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>3<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.7pt"> </SPAN></SPAN>日<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">，甲</SPAN>企业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">实</SPAN>际<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>到<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">补</SPAN>助<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">资</SPAN>金：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 115.5pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">银</SPAN>行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">存</SPAN>款<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">3</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0.1pt 235.05pt 6pt 0cm; tab-stops: 89.4pt" 
align=center><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT 
size=3>贷：<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">递</SPAN>延<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>益<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">3</SPAN>000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 26.1pt"><FONT size=3><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">(2)2<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">×</SPAN>18<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> 
</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">年～<SPAN

<H3 style="MARGIN: 13pt 0cm"><A name=_Toc72425509></A><A 
name=_Toc11952077></A><A name=_bookmark157></A><FONT size=5><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc72425509"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc11952077"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">六</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc72425509"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc11952077"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">、<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">关</SPAN>于特<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">定</SPAN>业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">务</SPAN>的会<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">计</SPAN>处理</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></H3>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.35pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 7pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 7pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_bookmark158></A><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（一）综合性项目<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">政</SPAN>府<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">补</SPAN>助的会计处理</SPAN><FONT face=Calibri> <SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">对于<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">同</SPAN>时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">包</SPAN>含<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">与</SPAN>资<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">产</SPAN>相<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">关</SPAN>部分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">和</SPAN>与<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>益<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">相</SPAN>关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">部</SPAN>分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的</SPAN>政府<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">补</SPAN>助<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">，</SPAN>企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">业</SPAN>应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">当</SPAN>将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">其</SPAN>进行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">分</SPAN>解<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">区</SPAN>分不同<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">部</SPAN>分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">分</SPAN>别<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">进</SPAN>行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">会</SPAN>计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">处</SPAN>理<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">；</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">难</SPAN>以<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">区</SPAN>分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">企</SPAN>业<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">应</SPAN>当将<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">其</SPAN>整<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">体</SPAN>归<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">类</SPAN>为<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">与</SPAN>收<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">益</SPAN>相关<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的</SPAN>政<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">府</SPAN>补<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">助进</SPAN>行会计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">处</SPAN>理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 11</SPAN>】<SPAN lang=EN-US>2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 6 
</SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 15 
</SPAN>日，某市科技创新委员会与乙企业签订了科技计划项目合同书，拟对乙企业的新药临床研究项目提供研究补助资金。该项目总预算为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 600 </SPAN>万元，其中，市科技创新委员会资助<SPAN lang=EN-US> 200 
</SPAN>万元，乙企业自筹<SPAN lang=EN-US> 400 </SPAN>万元。市科技创新委员会资助的<SPAN lang=EN-US> 200 
</SPAN>万元用于补助设备费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 60 </SPAN>万元，材料费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 15 
</SPAN>万元，测试化验加工费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 95 </SPAN>万元，差旅费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 
</SPAN>万元，会议费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5 </SPAN>万元，专家咨询费<SPAN lang=EN-US> 8 
</SPAN>万元，管理费用<SPAN lang=EN-US> 7 
</SPAN>万元，假设除设备费外的其他各项费用都属于研究支出。市科技创新委员会应当在合同签订之日起<SPAN lang=EN-US> 30 
</SPAN>日内将资金拨付给乙企业。根据双方约定，乙企业应当按合同规 
定的开支范围，对市科技创新委员会资助的经费实行专款专用。项目实施期限为自合同签订之日起<SPAN lang=EN-US> 30 
</SPAN>个月，期满后乙企业如未通过验收，在该项目实施期满后<SPAN lang=EN-US> 3 
</SPAN>年内不得再向市政府申请科技补贴资金。乙企业于<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 7 
</SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 </SPAN>日收到补助资金，在项目期内按照合同约定的用途使用了补助资金。乙企业于<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2×l7 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 7 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 25 
</SPAN>日按项目合同书的约定购置了相关设备，设备成本<SPAN lang=EN-US> 150 </SPAN>万元，其中使用补助资金<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 60 </SPAN>万元，该设备使用年限为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 </SPAN>年，采用直线法计提折旧（不考虑净残值） 
。假设本例中不考虑相关税费等其他因素。<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本例中，乙企业收到的政府补助是综合性项目政府补助，需要区分与资产相关的政府补助和与收益相关的政府补助并分别进行处理。假设乙企业对收到的与资产相关的政府补助选择净额法进行会计处理。乙企业的账务处理如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">(1)2×17 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 7 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 10 </SPAN>日乙企业实际收到补贴资金：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 115.5pt" 
align=left><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT 
size=3>借：<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">银</SPAN>行<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">存</SPAN>款<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText

      lang=EN-US

      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">银</SPAN>行<SPAN 
      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">存</SPAN>款<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 69.7pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly" 
    vAlign=top width=93>
      <P class=TableParagraph

  <TR style="HEIGHT: 15.6pt; mso-yfti-irow: 2; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 101.8pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly"

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 15.6pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 69.7pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly"

      <P class=TableParagraph

      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">600<SPAN 
      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">00</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR>
  <TR 
  style="HEIGHT: 18.1pt; mso-yfti-irow: 3; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-yfti-lastrow: yes">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 18.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 101.8pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly" 
    vAlign=top width=136>
      <P class=TableParagraph 
      style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 23pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.05pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">贷：<SPAN 
      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">固</SPAN>定<SPAN 
      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">资</SPAN>产<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 18.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #f0f0f0; WIDTH: 69.7pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: #f0f0f0; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly" 
    vAlign=top width=93>
      <P class=TableParagraph 
      style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 23.65pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.05pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">6</SPAN><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">000<SPAN 
      style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">0</SPAN>0<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD></TR></TBODY></TABLE></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0cm 15.6pt 6pt 26.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 10.6pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly" 
align=left><FONT size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">(3)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体">自<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>2×<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">l</SPAN>7<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt"> 
</SPAN></SPAN>年<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> </SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>8<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.65pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">月</SPAN>起<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">每个</SPAN>资产<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">负</SPAN>债<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">表</SPAN>日<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">折</SPAN>旧<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">费</SPAN>用<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">计</SPAN>入研<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">发</SPAN>支<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">出</SPAN>：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 115.5pt" 
align=left><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT 
size=3>借：<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">研</SPAN>发<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">支</SPAN>出<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">7</SPAN>500<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0.1pt 15.9pt 6pt 26.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; tab-stops: 136.5pt" 
align=left><SPAN style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT 
size=3>贷：<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">累</SPAN>计<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">折</SPAN>旧<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">7</SPAN>500 <o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">(4)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对其他与收益相关的政府补助，乙企业应当按照相关经济业务的实质确定是计入其他收益还是冲减相关成本费用，在企业按规定用途实际使用补助资金时计入损益，或者在实际使用的当期期末根据当期累计使用的金额计入损益，借记<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>递延收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>科目，贷记有关损益科目。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_bookmark159></A><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（二）政策性优惠贷款贴息的会计处理</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">政策性优惠贷款贴息是政府为支持特定领域或区域发展，根据国家宏观经济形势和政策目标，对承贷企业的银行借款利息给予的补贴。企业取得政策性优惠贷款贴息的，应当区分财政将贴息</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">资金拨付给贷款银行和财政将贴息资金直接拨付给企业两种情况，分别进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>1.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">财政将贴息资金拨付给贷款银行</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">在财政将贴息资金拨付给贷款银行的情况下，由贷款银行以政策性优惠利率向企业提供贷款。这种方式下，受益企业按照优惠利率向贷款银行支付利息，并没有直接从政府取得利息补助，企业可以选择下列方法之一进行会计处理：一是以实际收到的借款金额作为借款的入账价值，按照</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">借款本金和该政策性优惠利率计算相关借款费用。通常情况下，实际收到的金额即为借款本金。</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">二是以借款的公允价值作为借款的入账价值并按照实际利率法计算借款费用，实际收到的金额与</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">借款公允价值之间的差额确认为递延收益。递延收益在借款存续期内采用实际利率法摊销，冲减</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">相关借款费用。企业选择了上述两种方法之一后，应当一致地运用，不得随意变更。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">在这种情况下，向企业发放贷款的银行并不是受益主体，其仍然按照市场利率收取利息，只是一部分利息来自企业，另一部分利息来自财政贴息。所以贷款银行发挥的是中介作用，并不需要确认与贷款相关的递延收益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">【例<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 12</SPAN>】<SPAN lang=EN-US>2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
</SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>日，丙企业向银行贷款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 100 
</SPAN>万元，期限<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2 
</SPAN>年，按月计息，按季度付息，到期一次还本。这笔贷款资金将被用于国家扶持产业，符合财政贴息的条件，所以贷款利率显著低于丙企业取得同类贷款的市场利率。假设丙企业取得同类贷款的年市场利率为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 9%,</SPAN>丙企业与银行签订的贷款合同约定的年利率为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
3%</SPAN>，丙企业按季度向银行支付贷款利息，财政按年向银行拨付贴息资金。贴息后丙企业实际支付的年利息率为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
3%,</SPAN>贷款期间的利息费用满足资本化条件， 计入相关在建工程的成本。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 6pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 6pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P>

cellSpacing=0 cellPadding=0 border=0>

  <TR 
  style="HEIGHT: 17.1pt; mso-yfti-irow: 0; mso-yfti-firstrow: yes; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #dadcdd 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 17.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #dadcdd 1pt solid; WIDTH: 35.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #dadcdd 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt"

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #dadcdd 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 17.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #dadcdd 1pt solid; WIDTH: 335.55pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt"

      <P class=TableParagraph

      style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN">相关借款费用的计算和递延收益的摊销</SPAN><SPAN

    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #dadcdd 1pt solid; HEIGHT: 17.1pt; BORDER-RIGHT: #dadcdd 1pt solid; WIDTH: 64.6pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-bottom-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt"

  <TR style="HEIGHT: 34.15pt; mso-yfti-irow: 1; mso-height-rule: exactly">
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 35.9pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #dadcdd 1pt solid; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid #DADCDD .75pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .75pt" 
    vAlign=top width=48>
      <P class=TableParagraph 
      style="MARGIN: 0.15pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 8pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
      lang=EN-US style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><o:p><FONT 
      face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
      <P class=TableParagraph style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt 3.7pt"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">月度<o:p></o:p></SPAN></P></TD>
    <TD 
    style="BORDER-TOP: #f0f0f0; HEIGHT: 34.15pt; BORDER-RIGHT: black 1pt solid; WIDTH: 55.7pt; BORDER-BOTTOM: black 1pt solid; PADDING-BOTTOM: 0cm; PADDING-TOP: 0cm; PADDING-LEFT: 5.4pt; BORDER-LEFT: #f0f0f0; PADDING-RIGHT: 5.4pt; BACKGROUND-COLOR: transparent; mso-height-rule: exactly; mso-border-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-left-alt: solid black .75pt; mso-border-top-alt: solid black .75pt" 
    vAlign=top width=74>
      <P class=TableParagraph 
      style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0.3pt 3.7pt 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 11.4pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly" 
      align=center><SPAN 
      style="FONT-SIZE: 9.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-language: ZH-CN">按市场利率

<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 1.25pt 9.7pt 0pt 5.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 117%; TEXT-INDENT: 17.95pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 117%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">注：（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1)</SPAN>实际现金流折现<SPAN lang=EN-US>④</SPAN>为各月实际现金流<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>③2500 </SPAN>元按照月市场利率 <SPAN lang=EN-US>0.75%</SPAN>（<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>=9%÷12</SPAN>）折现的金额。例如，第一个月实际现金流折现<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>=2500÷(1+0.75%)=2481(</SPAN>元），第二个月实际现金流折现<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>=2500÷(1+0.75%) =2463(</SPAN>元）。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 1.25pt 9.7pt 0pt 5.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 117%; TEXT-INDENT: 17.95pt"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 117%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">(2)</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 117%; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体">长期借款各期实际利息<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>⑤</SPAN><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">为</SPAN>各月长期借款账面价值<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>⑦</SPAN>与月市场利率<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt"> </SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">0</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">.</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">7</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">5</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">%</SPAN>的乘积<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.95pt">。</SPAN>例如<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.05pt">，</SPAN>第一个月长期借 款实际利<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">息</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">=</SPAN>本月初长期借款账面价值<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt"> </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">8</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">9</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">0</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US

lang=EN-US>③2500</SPAN>元后的金额。例如，第一个月摊销金额<SPAN lang=EN-US>=</SPAN>当月长期借款实际利息

lang=EN-US>2500=4179(</SPAN>元），第二个月摊销金额<SPAN lang=EN-US>=</SPAN>当月长期借款实际利息 <SPAN 
lang=EN-US>6711-</SPAN>当月实际支付的利息 <SPAN lang=EN-US>2500=4211(</SPAN>元）。<SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 10.6pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>同时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">，</SPAN>摊<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">销</SPAN>递<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">延</SPAN>收<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">益</SPAN>：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 110.2pt"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>借：<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">递</SPAN>延<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>益<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </SPAN>4<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">1</SPAN>79<o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">贷：在建工程<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> 
</SPAN>4179<o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 1.05pt 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 15.6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt; mso-line-height-rule: exactly"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">在上述两种方法下，丙企业每月计入在建工程的利息支出是一致的，均为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2500 </SPAN>元。不同的是，在方法一下，丙企业该笔银行贷款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>日长期借款的账面价值为<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 1000000 </SPAN>元；在方法二下，丙企业该笔银行贷款<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2×17 </SPAN>年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>日长期借款的账面价值为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 
890554 </SPAN>元，此外还有递延收益<SPAN lang=EN-US> 109446 </SPAN>元，各月需要按照实际利率法对递延收益进行摊销。 
<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">财政将贴息资金直接拨付给企业</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">财政将贴息资金直接拨付给受益企业，企业先按照同类贷款市场利率向银行支付利息，财政部门定期与企业结算贴息。在这种方式下，由于企业先按照同类贷款市场利率向银行支付利息，</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">所以实际收到的借款金额通常就是借款的公允价值，企业应当将对应的贴息冲减相关借款费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 4.35pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 100%; TEXT-INDENT: 20.95pt"><SPAN

<P class=MsoBodyText

style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">0</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">(</SPAN></SPAN>元<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -5.4pt">）</SPAN>，应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">收</SPAN>政<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">府</SPAN>贴<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">息</SPAN>为<SPAN lang=EN-US> 5000<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.75pt"> </SPAN></SPAN>元：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt 26.1pt; tab-stops: 110.05pt"><SPAN

<H3 style="MARGIN: 1.3pt 0cm 13pt"><A name=_Toc72425510></A><A 
name=_Toc11952078></A><A name=_bookmark160></A><FONT size=5><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc72425510"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc11952078"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">七</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc72425510"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Toc11952078"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">、<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">关</SPAN>于政<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">府</SPAN>补<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">助</SPAN>的列报</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></H3>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_bookmark161></A><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（一）政府补助在利润表上的列示</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">企业应当在利润表中的</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">营业利润</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项目之上单独列报</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">其他收益</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项目，计入其他收益的政府补助在该项目中反映。冲减相关成本费用的政府补助，在相关成本费用项目中反映。与企业</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日常经营活动无关的政府补助，在利润表的营业外收支项目中反映。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p><FONT size=3 face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><A 
name=_bookmark162></A><FONT size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">（二）政府补助在财务报表附注中的披露</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">因政府补助涉及递延收益、其他收益、营业外收入以及相关成本费用等多个报表项目，为了全面反映政府补助情况，企业应当在附注中单独披露政府补助的相关信息。本准则规定，企业应当在附注中单独披露与政府补助有关的下列信息：政府补助的种类、金额和列报项目；计入当期</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">损益的政府补助金额；本期退回的政府补助金额及原因。其中，列报项目不仅包括总额法下计入其他收益、营业外收入、递延收益等项目，还包括净额法下冲减的资产和成本费用等项目。</SPAN></FONT><A 
name=_bookmark163></A><SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<H3 style="MARGIN: 1.3pt 0cm 13pt"><A name=_Toc72425511></A><A 
name=_Toc11952079><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Toc72425511"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin"><FONT 
size=5>八、关于新旧准则的衔接规定</FONT></SPAN></SPAN></A><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></H3>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">本准则规定，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2006 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>15 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日财政部印发的《财政部关于印发〈企业会计准则第</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">存货〉等</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>38 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">项具体准则的通知》中的《企业会计准则第</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>16 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">政府补助》同时废止。企业对</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2017 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日存在的政府补助采用未来适用法处理，对</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日至本准则施行日之间</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">新增的政府补助根据本准则进行调整。财政部此前发布的有关政府补助会计处理规定与本准则不</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">一致的，以本准则为准。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><FONT 
size=3><SPAN lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2017 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日存在的政府补助主要指当日仍存在尚未分摊计入损益的与政府补助有关的递延收益。因采用未来适用法，企业不需调整</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2016 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>31 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日有关科目的期末余额，在编制</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年年报时也不需调整可比期间的比较数据。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><FONT face=Calibri>2017 </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日至本准则施行日之间新增的政府补助，主要指在这一期间内新取得的政府补助。企业对</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日存在的和</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日至本准则施行日之间新增的政府补助应当视同从</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">月</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">日起按照政府补助准则进行会计处理，以确保在</SPAN><FONT 
face=Calibri> <SPAN lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin">年度对政府补助业务采用的会计处理方法保持一致。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 6pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt; mso-char-indent-count: 2.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: 楷体"><FONT size=3>【例<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.5pt"> </SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">4</SPAN></SPAN>】<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">丁</SPAN>企<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">业</SPAN>于<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.5pt"> 
</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US>2<SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">0</SPAN>1<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">7 </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
</SPAN>日存在尚未摊销的递延收益（与资产相关的政府补助）<SPAN lang=EN-US>50</SPAN>万元，该项递延收益对应的固定资产原值是 
<SPAN lang=EN-US>400 
</SPAN>万元。根据本准则的衔接规定，丁企业在本准则施行后有两种处理方法：一是继续采用总额法，在这种方法下无需调整固定资产原值和递延收益， 
但需要根据本准则对递延收益应当计入<SPAN lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>其他收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>还是<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>营业外收入<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>进行判断，如果判断应当计入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>其他收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>，则将<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2017 
</SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>日以来摊销的递延收益从<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>营业外收入<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>中转出计入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>其他收益<SPAN lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>。二是选择采用净额法，将递延收益在<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 2017 </SPAN>年<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US> 1 
</SPAN>日的余额冲减相关固定资产原值（原值调整为 <SPAN lang=EN-US>350 
</SPAN>万元），并以调整后的固定资产账面价值为基础计提折旧，同时调整自<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2017 </SPAN>年<SPAN 
lang=EN-US> 1 </SPAN>月<SPAN lang=EN-US>1 </SPAN>日起因摊销该项递延收益而计入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>“</SPAN>营业外收入<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>”</SPAN>的金额以及相关资产计提的折旧费用。需要强调的是，企业不需调整<SPAN lang=EN-US> 2016 </SPAN>年 
<SPAN lang=EN-US>12 </SPAN>月 <SPAN lang=EN-US>31 </SPAN>日有关资产负债的期末余额，在编制 <SPAN 
lang=EN-US>2017 </SPAN>年年报时也不 需调整可比期间的比较数据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
